It features several decrees from the Amir and Prime Minister concerning diplomatic transfers and ministerial substitutions, alongside ministerial decisions on identifying ultimate beneficial owners and granting capital market licenses. The gazette also includes numerous tender announcements from various ministries and public authorities for projects ranging from infrastructure and military supplies to sports facility maintenance and oil sector services. Additionally, it publishes official announcements regarding company registrations, liquidations, changes in legal status, and public auctions for vehicles, real estate, and other seized goods, concluding with criminal judgments, legal notices, and corrections to personal data.",

# Decree No. 35 of 2025
## Regarding the Transfer of Some Heads of Diplomatic Missions to the General Diwan of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH, corresponding to May 10, 2024 AD,
- And Law No. 21 of 1962 regarding the Diplomatic and Consular Corps System, and its amending laws,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Foreign Affairs,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers,

We have decreed the following:

### Article One

The following heads of diplomatic missions shall be transferred to the General Diwan of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs:
1.

  1. Mansour Saad Al-Olaymi <orig>منصور سعد العليمي</orig>, Ambassador of the State of Kuwait to the Hellenic Republic.
  2. Thiab Farhan Al-Rashidi <orig>ذياب فرحان الرشيدي</orig>, Ambassador of the State of Kuwait to the Republic of Korea.
  3. Khalid Bader Al-Mutairi <orig>خالد بدر المطيري</orig>, Ambassador of the State of Kuwait to the State of Qatar.

### Article Two

The Minister of Foreign Affairs shall implement this Decree, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

# Council of Ministers
## Decree No. 34 of 2025
### Amending Decree No. 84 of 2024 Regarding Ministerial Substitutions and Delegations

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to May 10, 2024 AD,
- And Decree No. 73 of 2024 regarding the formation of the Ministry, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 84 of 2024 regarding ministerial substitutions and delegations, and its amending decrees,
- And based on the submission of the Prime Minister,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers,

We have decreed the following:

### Article One

Item (1) of Article Two of Decree No. 84 of 2024, as amended by Decree No. 164 of 2024, shall be replaced with the following text:
((1) - The First Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Interior shall perform the duties of the Minister of Defense during his absence.))
The Minister of Defense shall perform the duties of the Minister of Interior during his absence.

### Article Two

The Prime Minister and the Ministers - each within his respective jurisdiction - shall implement this Decree, and anything contrary thereto shall be repealed. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

Amir of Kuwait
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>

Prime Minister
Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>

Minister of Foreign Affairs
Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Yahya <orig>عبد الله علي عبد الله اليحيا</orig>

Issued at Seif Palace on: 24 Sha'ban 1446 AH
Corresponding to February 23, 2025 AD

# Decree No. 36 of 2025
## Regarding the Transfer of Ministers Plenipotentiary
## To the General Diwan of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhul-Qa'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And Law No. 21 of 1962 regarding the Diplomatic and Consular Corps System <orig>نظام السلكين الدبلوماسي والقنصلي</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزير الخارجية</orig>,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,
**We have decreed the following:**
**Article One**
The following shall be transferred to the General Diwan of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزارة الخارجية</orig>:
1 – Abdullah Yousef Al-Hailam <orig>عبد الله يوسف الهيلم</orig>, Minister Plenipotentiary <orig>الوزير المفوض</orig> at the Consulate General of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> to the United States of America <orig>الولايات المتحدة الأمريكية</orig> in Los Angeles <orig>لوس أنجلس</orig>.
2 – Khalid Salman Al-Kharij <orig>خالد سلمان الخريج</orig>, Minister Plenipotentiary <orig>الوزير المفوض</orig> at the Embassy of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> to the Republic of Armenia <orig>جمهورية أرمينيا</orig>.
3 – Khalid Hamad Al-Khalidi <orig>خالد حمد الخالدي</orig>, Minister Plenipotentiary <orig>الوزير المفوض</orig> at the Embassy of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> to the Republic of South Africa <orig>جمهورية جنوب أفريقيا</orig>.
**Article Two**
The Minister of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزير الخارجية</orig> shall implement this Decree, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

**Amir of Kuwait**
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>

**Prime Minister**
Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>

**Minister of Foreign Affairs**
Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Yahya <orig>عبد الله علي عبد الله اليحيا</orig>

Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 24 Sha'ban 1446 AH
Corresponding to 23 February 2025 AD

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Ministerial Decision No. (16) of 2025 Amending Ministerial Decision No. (4) of 2023 Regarding Procedures for Identifying the Ultimate Beneficial Owner <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (16) لسنة 2025 بتعديل بعض أحكام القرار الوزاري رقم (4) لسنة 2023 بشأن إجراءات تحديد هوية المستفيد الفعلي</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-03-02",
  "issue_number": 1728,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>",
  "publisher": "Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page details Ministerial Decision No. (16) of 2025, which amends Decision No. (4) of 2023 concerning procedures for identifying the ultimate beneficial owner, outlining the legal basis, scope of application, and required registration data for legal entities in Kuwait."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
4
</header>

- The proposal submitted by the Undersecretary <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig>,
- And based on the requirements of public interest,
- And pursuant to the powers vested in us.
Has decided:
**Article One**
The texts of Articles (3), (4), and (17) of Ministerial Resolution No. (4) of 2023 shall be replaced with the following texts:
**Article (3):**
The provisions of this Resolution shall apply to all legal persons registered in the State, with the following exceptions:
1.  Companies wholly owned by the Government of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> or a foreign government.
2.  Legal entities listed on local and international stock exchanges and subject to disclosure requirements that ensure sufficient transparency of beneficial ownership, as well as their majority-owned subsidiaries.
3.  Investment entities licensed in accordance with Law No. 116 of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم 116 لسنة 2013</orig> referred to, provided that they submit disclosure of beneficial owner data within three months from the date of issuance of the commercial license in accordance with the procedures specified by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
**Article (4):**
Any legal person in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, as part of its registration process, must submit the following basic data to the Registrar <orig>المسجل</orig>:
a) The name of the legal person, its legal form, and its legal status, along with a copy of the articles of incorporation.
b) The address of the head office or principal place of business, and if the legal person is a foreign entity, the name and address of its legal representative in the State must be registered.
c) A copy of the articles of incorporation or any other similar documents approved by the competent authority in Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig>.
d) The names of all relevant persons holding senior management positions in the legal person, including passport document data or civil ID number, and dates of issue and expiry.

- Penal Code <orig>قانون الجزاء</orig> issued by Law No. (16) of 1960 <orig>القانون رقم (16) لسنة 1960</orig> and its amendments,
- Code of Criminal Procedures and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig> issued by Law No. (17) of 1960 <orig>القانون رقم (17) لسنة 1960</orig> and its amendments,
- Law No. (32) of 1968 <orig>القانون رقم (32) لسنة 1968</orig> concerning Currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, and the Regulation of the Money Exchange Profession, and its amendments,
- Law No. (7) of 2010 <orig>القانون رقم (7) لسنة 2010</orig> concerning the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities, and its amendments,
- Law No. (106) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (106) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning Combating Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing, amended by Law No. (24) of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم (24) لسنة 2016</orig>,
- Law No. (111) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (111) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning Commercial Licenses,
- Law No. (116) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (116) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning the Encouragement of Direct Investment in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>,
- Law No. (1) of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم (1) لسنة 2016</orig> concerning the Issuance of the Companies Law and its amendments,
- Law No. (2) of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم (2) لسنة 2016</orig> concerning the Establishment of the Public Anti-Corruption Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة لمكافحة الفساد</orig> and Provisions for Financial Disclosure,
- Law No. (18) of 2018 <orig>القانون رقم (18) لسنة 2018</orig> concerning the Commercial Register,
- Law No. (125) of 2019 <orig>القانون رقم (125) لسنة 2019</orig> concerning the Regulation of Insurance,
- Decree No. (191) of 2015 <orig>المرسوم رقم (191) لسنة 2015</orig> concerning the Organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>,
- Decree No. (300) of 2016 <orig>المرسوم رقم (300) لسنة 2016</orig> issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (2) of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم (2) لسنة 2016</orig> concerning the Establishment of the Public Anti-Corruption Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة لمكافحة الفساد</orig> and Financial Disclosure,
- Decree No. (73) of 2024 <orig>المرسوم رقم (73) لسنة 2024</orig> concerning the Formation of the Government and its amendments,
- Ministerial Resolution No. (37) of 2013 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (37) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning the Issuance of the Executive Regulations for Law No. (106) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (106) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning Combating Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing, and its amendments,
- Ministerial Resolution No. (411) of 2013 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (411) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning the Issuance of the Executive Regulations for Law No. (111) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (111) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning Commercial Licenses, and its amendments,
- Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> Resolution No. (72) of 2015 <orig>قرار هيئة أسواق المال رقم (72) لسنة 2015</orig> issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (7) of 2010 <orig>القانون رقم (7) لسنة 2010</orig> concerning the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities, and its amendments,

  "page_title": "Decision No. (35) of 2025 regarding a special marketing license for a collective investment scheme established outside the State of Kuwait granted to Bayt Al-Awraq Financial for marketing units of Laverne Industrial Real Estate Fund <orig>قرار رقم (35) لسنة 2025 بشأن رخصة تسويق خاص لنظام استثمار جماعي مؤسس خارج دولة الكويت ممنوحة لشركة بيت الأوراق المالية لتسويق وحدات صندوق لافيرن للعقار الصناعي</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-02-18",
  "issue_number": 1728,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": ["ar", "en", "mixed"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Minister of Commerce and Industry / Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajeel <orig>وزير التجارة والصناعة خليفة عبدالله العجيل</orig>",
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page details Decision No. (35) of 2025 by the Capital Markets Authority, granting Bayt Al-Awraq Financial a license to market 6,000 units of the Laverne Industrial Real Estate Fund, outlining the fund's composition, unit price, subscription fees, and additional provisions regarding legal entity registration and penalties for non-compliance."

</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
5
</header>

It was decided as follows:

### Article One
Al-Bait Securities Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> is licensed to privately market 6,000 units (six thousand units only) of the LA VERGNE INDUSTRIAL REAL ESTATE FUND within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, established in the Cayman Islands. Each unit consists of the following:
1. One (1) ordinary share, the holder of which has voting rights in Phoenix Real Estate Company Limited <orig>شركة فينيكس للعقار المحدودة</orig>.
2. Three (3) ordinary shares, the holder of which has voting rights in Phoenix Finance Company Limited <orig>شركة فينيكس للتمويل المحدودة</orig>.
The offer price shall be 4,000 US Dollars (four thousand US Dollars only) per unit, in addition to a subscription commission of 0.1% of the offer price upon subscription.

### Additional Provisions:
1. A legal entity may not be registered or licensed under a name previously registered in the State or under a similar name that may cause confusion.
2. The legal entity must refrain from using any name other than its registered name, provided that the name is followed by the legal form of the entity. The legal entity may also apply to the registrar for a name change, and if approved, the old name may not be used immediately upon its cancellation.
3. All correspondence and documents must clearly include the name of the legal entity and its registered address in the State.

### Article (16)
Without prejudice to any harsher penalties stipulated in Law No. (106) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (106) لسنة 2013</orig> and other relevant legislation, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> has the right to impose the following penalties on any legal entity that fails to comply with its obligations under this decision, including failure to maintain, register, or update the required beneficial owner data:
1. Warning.
2. An administrative fine of not less than 1,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and not exceeding 10,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> for each violation.
3. Suspension of company registration for up to three months.
If the violation continues for more than three months after suspension, the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> may apply to the court for the final delisting of the legal entity from the commercial register.

### Article (17)
No license may be granted or renewed unless the requirements of this decision are met. Administrative fines ranging from a minimum of 1,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> to a maximum of 10,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> shall be imposed for each violation, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (106) of 2013 <orig>القانون رقم (106) لسنة 2013</orig> concerning Combating Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing <orig>مكافحة غسل الأموال وتمويل الإرهاب</orig>, its executive regulations, and amendments, in the event of non-disclosure of the beneficial owner.

### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

<footer>
Issued on: 19 Sha'ban 1446 AH
Corresponding to: 18 February 2025 AD
Minister of Commerce and Industry
Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajeel <orig>خليفة عبدالله العجيل</orig>

# Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>
## Administrative Decision No. 28/2025 GM Regarding the Suspension of the Engineering Office / Saleh Abdulghani Al-Mutawa Engineering Consultations <orig>صالح عبد الغني المطوع للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> – Owned by Engineer / Saleh Abdulghani Abdulredha Al-Mutawa <orig>صالح عبد الغني عبد الرضا المطوع</orig>
Director General of the Municipality
- Having reviewed Law No. (33/2016) concerning Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> and its amendments.
- Having reviewed Ministerial Decision No. (123/2021) issuing the Professional Practice Regulations for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>المكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig> and its amendments.
- Having reviewed Ministerial Decision No. (363/2009) concerning the organization of the Municipality's Executive Body <orig>الجهاز التنفيذي للبلدية</orig> and its branches in the governorates.
- Having reviewed Ministerial Decision No. (206/2009) concerning the regulation of construction works and its annexed schedules dated 30/4/2009 and its amendments.
- Having reviewed Administrative Decision No. (A781/2024) dated 27/5/2024 regarding the re-formation of the Committee for Regulating Professional Practice for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>لجنة تنظيم مزاولة المهنة للمكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig>.
- Having reviewed Administrative Decision No. (374/2021) dated 25/10/2021 regarding the renewal of the engineering office's registration.
- Having reviewed the letter from the Committee for Professional Practice for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>لجنة مزاولة المهنة للمكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig> No. (00019-2024) dated 5/12/2024.
- Having reviewed the Committee's recommendation at its meeting No. (12/2024) held on 3/12/2024 regarding the suspension of the engineering office.
Has decided:
### Article One
Approval of the Committee's recommendation taken at meeting No. (12/2024) dated 3/12/2024 to suspend the engineering office – a temporary suspension (for a period of 9 months) of the office / Saleh Abdulghani Al-Mutawa Engineering Consultations <orig>صالح عبد الغني المطوع للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> owned by Engineer / Saleh Abdulghani Abdulredha Al-Mutawa <orig>صالح عبد الغني عبد الرضا المطوع</orig> – this is based on the text of Article (29) of Ministerial Decision No. (123/2021), provided that it commences from the date of expiry of the penalty issued under Administrative Decision No. (1/2025) dated 14/1/2024.
### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, and it shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.
Director General of the Municipality
Issued on 23 February 2025 AD

### Article Two
The units to be marketed within the State of Kuwait shall be offered to professional clients only, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 concerning the Establishment of Capital Markets and the Regulation of Securities Activities <orig>أسواق المال وتنظيم نشاط الأوراق المالية</orig> and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription requests shall be:
- Securities House Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig>.
### Article Three
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.
### Article Four
The marketing license duration is one year, renewable annually, starting from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.
### Article Five
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the decision shall be considered null and void.
### Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction, and it shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.
Head of Supervision Sector
Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>
Issued on 23 February 2025 AD

2.  Bids shall be placed in the designated box in the Procurement and Warehouses Department at the Ministry of Public Works <orig>وزارة الأشغال العامة</orig> no later than 1:00 PM on Sunday, 23/03/2025, and any bid submitted after this deadline will be rejected.
3.  The initial security deposit shall not be less than (2%) and not exceed (5%) of the total value of the bidder's offer, and this guarantee must be valid throughout the validity period of the offer.
4.  The final security deposit is: (15%) of the total contract value, provided that the value of the final security deposit exceeds or equals the value of any due payments, taking into account that the final security deposit shall be adjusted in case of any changes to the contract value, whether by increase or decrease, during its execution.
5.  The license period is: two full calendar years, starting from the date to be specified in the written commencement order that will be issued to the bidder after the contract is signed by both parties.
6.  The bid shall remain valid for 90 days (ninety days) from the date of opening the bid envelopes.
7.  Partial bidding is not allowed.
8.  Alternative offers are not accepted.

# Administrative Decision No. 29 GM 2025 / Regarding the Suspension of Palmyra Engineering Consultations <orig>بالميرا للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> – Owned by Engineer / Mohammed Hussein Ali Hassan Al-Sayegh <orig>محمد حسين علي حسن الصايغ</orig>

Director General of the Municipality <orig>مدير عام البلدية</orig>
*   Upon reviewing Law No. (33/2016) concerning Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> and its amendments.
*   Upon Ministerial Decision No. (123/2021) issuing the Professional Practice Regulations for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>المكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig> and its amendments.
*   Upon Ministerial Decision No. (363/2009) concerning the organization of the Municipality's Executive Apparatus <orig>الجهاز التنفيذي للبلدية</orig> and its branches in the governorates.
*   Upon Ministerial Decision No. (206/2009) concerning the regulation of construction works and its annexed schedules dated 30/4/2009 and its amendments.
*   Upon Administrative Decision No. (A2024/781) dated 27/5/2024 concerning the re-formation of the Committee for Regulating Professional Practice for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>لجنة تنظيم مزاولة المهنة للمكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig>.
*   Upon Administrative Decision No. (185/2021) dated 3/6/2021 concerning the qualification of the engineering office as a consulting firm.
*   Upon the letter from the Committee for Professional Practice for Engineering Offices and Consulting Firms <orig>لجنة مزاولة المهنة للمكاتب الهندسية والدور الاستشارية</orig> No. (00002 – 2025) dated 13/1/2025.
*   Upon the Committee's recommendation in its meeting No. (1/2025) held on 7/1/2025 regarding the temporary suspension of the engineering firm.
    – Has Decided –

### Article One
Approval of the recommendation of the Joint Committee <orig>اللجنة المتحدة</orig> in its meeting No. (1/2025) held on 7/1/2025 to temporarily suspend Palmyra Engineering Consultations <orig>بالميرا للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> – owned by Engineer / Mohammed Hussein Ali Hassan Al-Sayegh <orig>محمد حسين علي حسن الصايغ</orig> – from supervision activities (for a period of 6 months) – based on the text of Article (29) of Ministerial Decision No. (123/2021).

### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, and it shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

The final performance bond is: (15%) of the total contract value, provided that the value of the final performance bond exceeds or equals the value of any due payments, taking into account that the final performance bond shall be adjusted in case of any changes to the contract value, whether by increase or decrease, during its execution.

Whether the bidder attends this preliminary meeting or not, they shall be considered fully aware of the condition of sand on the roads and fully informed of all decisions, directives, and recommendations taken in this meeting, whether before or after the conclusion of the contract.
11. The bid must be accompanied by a clearance certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating that the bidder is clear of consumption debts.
12. The bid must be accompanied by a certificate of payment of subscriptions to the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> as stipulated in Article (95) of the Social Security Law <orig>قانون التأمينات الاجتماعية</orig>.
13. The bid must be accompanied by a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority.
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Public Works <orig>وكيل وزارة الأشغال العامة</orig>

* The Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig> will hold a preliminary meeting on Sunday, 9 March 2025, at 11:00 AM in the meeting room of the Assistant Undersecretary for Engineering Affairs – Information Complex / Mujamma' Al-I'lam <orig>مجمع الإعلام</orig> – Al-Sour Street <orig>شارع السور</orig>, to answer inquiries submitted regarding the tender. Anyone who has purchased the tender documents may attend the meeting in person or be represented by another. Everything recorded in the meeting minutes shall be considered an integral part of the tender documents and shall be binding on bidders. The Ministry will circulate the questions, inquiries, and their approved responses to all tenderers before the tender closing date.
* All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, 3 copies, except for:
1. Tender form (hard copy).
2. Preliminary bond (hard copy).
3. Copy of purchase receipt (hard copy).
4. Tenderer's data form (hard copy).
* The tender is indivisible, and alternative offers will not be accepted.
* This announcement serves as an invitation for tenderers wishing to attend the bid opening session, after coordinating with the Procurement Department / Idarat Al-Mushtariyat <orig>إدارة المشتريات</orig> before the specified date for the bid opening session.
* The bidder must attach a valid national labor fulfillment certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Quwa Al-Amila <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> with the bid, noting that bids not including this certificate will be excluded.
* The bidder must attach a valid "to whom it may concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Quwa Al-Amila <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the tenderer's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 concerning labor in the private sector, noting that bids not including this certificate will be excluded.
* The bidder must attach a certificate of payment of subscriptions to the Public Institution for Social Security / Al-Mu'assasa Al-Amma Lil-Ta'minat Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> as stipulated in Article 95 of the Social Insurance Law / Qanun Al-Ta'minat Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>قانون التأمينات الاجتماعية</orig>.
* Owners of small and medium enterprises (SMEs) are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Article 39 of Law No. 74 of 2019 regarding amendments to Law No. 49 of 2016.
* Owners of small and medium enterprises wishing to apply for the tender must attach with their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development / Al-Sundooq Al-Watani Li-Ri'ayat wa Tanmiyat Al-Mashroo'at Al-Saghira wal-Mutawassita <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming its accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
* This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.
* To obtain a copy, the tenderer must register and pay fees through the website https://eservice.media.gov.kw/purchase

## Ministry of Commerce and Industry / Wizarat Al-Tijara wal-Sina'a <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
### Announcement

The esteemed owners of Atifelder United General Trading Company <orig>شركة اتيفلدر المتحددة للتجارة العامة</orig> (Company under liquidation) have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships / Idarat Sharikat Al-Ashkhas <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry to carry out the dissolution and liquidation of the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court / Al-Mahkama Al-Kulliya <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the jointly liable partners, in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until their objection is decided by a judicial ruling.

Announcement
The owners of Binank Tower Retail Company for Electrical Tools and its affiliates <orig>بينانك تاور للبيع بالتجزئة للأدوات الكهربائية ومقيداتها</orig> ## Company under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out: Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

The submission of an objection results in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

## Secondly: Unanimous Approval of Attendees to Amend the Text of Article 25 of the Articles of Association to Read as Follows:

The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall carry out all operations required for the management of the Company and its branches, in accordance with its objectives. This authority shall only be limited by what is stipulated by law, these Articles of Association, or the resolutions of the General Assembly. The Board of Directors shall have full authority to sell the Company's real estate, borrow, request banking facilities, accept their terms and conditions, and sign all their documents, undertakings, declarations, and renewals, including issuing/drafting promissory notes and all necessary documents for them, providing guarantees and sureties on behalf of the Company and its branches inside and outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, and all types of mortgages, including mortgaging the Company's real estate and its branches, concluding guarantees, accepting arbitration and conciliation, and making donations, both inside and outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, within the limits required by the Company's interest. The Board of Directors may delegate all or part of its powers to one or more of its members or to third parties.

## Thirdly: Unanimous Approval of Attendees to Amend the Text of Article (46) of the Articles of Association to Read as Follows:

## Net profits shall be distributed as follows:

*   **First:** 10% (ten percent) shall be deducted and allocated to the statutory reserve account. The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية</orig> may cease this deduction if the statutory reserve exceeds half of the Company's capital.
*   **Second:** Annually, by a resolution issued by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, a percentage not exceeding 10% (ten percent) of the net profits may be deducted to form a special reserve for purposes determined by the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>.
*   **Third:** 1% of the Company's annual profits shall be deducted for the benefit of the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig> and paid to the Foundation, in accordance with the Amiri Decree issued on December 12, 1976.
*   **Fourth:** A portion of the profits, determined by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>, shall be deducted to meet the Company's obligations under labor and social insurance laws, and may not be distributed

Fifth: The Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>, based on the Board of Directors' <orig>مجلس الادارة</orig> proposal, may distribute profits to shareholders at the end of the fiscal year. For this distribution to be valid, it must be from real profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and must not affect the company's paid-up capital.
Accordingly, the company's Board of Directors <orig>مجلس ادارة الشركة</orig> was instructed to take the necessary measures to register the approved amendments to the company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الاساسي</orig> in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig>.
The meeting was adjourned at 12:30 PM.

# United Kuwaiti Investments Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الاستثمارات الكويتية المتحدة ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting for the Fiscal Year Ended 31 December 2024
The Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> of the shareholders of United Kuwaiti Investments Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الاستثمارات الكويتية المتحدة ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> held its ordinary meeting at 10:30 AM on Wednesday, 12 February 2025, in Sharq – Khalid Ibn Al-Waleed Street <orig>شارع خالد ابن الوليد</orig> – KIPCO Tower <orig>برج كيبكو</orig> – 49th Floor. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Farouk Taha Abdul Latif Al-Oumi <orig>فاروق طه عبد اللطيف العومي</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>. The following also attended the meeting:
- Dr. Ali Owaid Rakhees <orig>علي عويد رخيص</orig> – Company Auditor from Al-Waha Auditing Office <orig>مكتب الواحة لتدقيق الحسابات</orig>.
- And shareholders representing 50,000,000 shares, in person and by proxy, of the company's capital shares, representing a 100% attendance rate.
After the announcement of the quorum being met, Mr. Farouk Taha Abdul Latif Al-Oumi <orig>فاروق طه بعداللطيف العومي</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> and Chairman of the Session – opened the meeting, welcoming the attendees. Subsequently, the items on the agenda were reviewed and discussed, and the following was approved:
The company's Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> reviewed the agenda and made the following decisions:
Item One: Approval was granted for the increase of the company's authorized, issued, and paid-up capital from K.D. 5,000,000 (Five Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) to K.D. 17,000,000 (Seventeen Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), an increase of K.D. 12,000,000 (Twelve Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), with a share value of 100 fils, as a cash increase payable in one installment, allocated to existing shareholders, with authorization to the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> to set the controls, rules, and conditions for calling up capital and disposing of fractional shares, if any.
Item Two: Approval was granted for the amendment of Article (6) of the Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (5) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>, so that the text of the article becomes as follows:
### Text Before Amendment:
The company's capital was set at K.D. 5,000,000 (Five Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over 50,000,000 (Fifty Million) shares, with a value of 100 fils per share, and all shares are cash shares.
### Text After Amendment:
The company's authorized and issued capital was set at K.D. 17,000,000 (Seventeen Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over 170,000,000 (One Hundred Seventy Million) shares, with a value of 100 fils per share, and all shares are cash shares.
The company's paid-up capital was set at K.D. 5,000,000 (Five Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over 50,000,000 (Fifty Million) shares, with a value of 100 fils per share, and all shares are cash shares.
Before the end of the meeting, the Chairman of the Session thanked the attendees and concluded the proceedings of the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> meeting at 11:00 AM on the same day.
Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> and Chairman of the Session

# Al-Tafawuq Holding Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة التفوق القابضة ش.م.ك ( مقفلة )</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
The Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> of Al-Tafawuq Holding Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة التفوق القابضة ش.م.ك ( مقفلة )</orig> held its meeting on Wednesday, 19 February 2025, at 12:00 PM at the company's headquarters in Al-Mirqab <orig>المرقاب</orig> – Kuwait Business City Real Estate Tower <orig>برج مدينة الاعمال الكويتية العقارية</orig> – 25th Floor – Meeting Room.
The meeting was attended by:
1- Mr. Abdulaziz Abdullah Al-Baloul <orig>عبدالعزيز عبدالله البالول</orig>
Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> – Chairman of the Meeting Session
2- Mr. Bahaa Salah Taher <orig>بهاء صلاح طاهر</orig>
Board Secretary
3- Mr. Abdulaziz Abdullah Al-Baghli <orig>عبدالعزيز عبدالله البغلي</orig>
Minority Shareholders' Representative
4- Shareholders holding 459,937,914 shares by proxy, representing 91.02% of the company's total shares, which amount to 202,753,460 shares.
After the announcement of the legal quorum being met for the valid convening of the (adjourned) Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية غير العادية</orig> meeting, Mr. Abdulaziz Abdullah Al-Baloul <orig>عبدالعزيز عبدالله البالول</orig> opened the meeting session, welcoming the attendees. He then proceeded to present the item on the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig>, and the following was decided:
First: Approval was granted for the proposed amendments to the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> and subsequent amendments:
### Item One: Amendment of Article (14) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>
#### Text Before Amendment
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (3) three members, and the term of membership shall be three years, renewable.
If a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> cannot be elected by the specified date, the existing Board shall continue to manage the company's affairs until the reasons cease to exist and a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> is elected.
The company may have a Chief Executive Officer <orig>رئيسا تنفيذيا</orig> appointed by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> from among its members or others, entrusted with the management of the company. The Board shall determine his allowances and powers to sign on behalf of the company.
#### Text After Amendment
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (5) five members, from whom the entity or entities entitled to second representatives to the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall appoint members in proportion to their shareholding in the company, and the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> shall elect the remaining members by secret ballot.
Provided that the Board includes one or more independent members who meet the conditions required by regulatory authorities and possess qualifications, experience, and skills commensurate with the company's activity. These members shall be chosen by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>, and their remuneration shall be determined according to governance rules, provided that their number does not exceed half of the Board members. It is not required for an independent member to be among the company's shareholders, and it should be noted that the term of membership for an independent member ends with the expiry of the Board's term for which they were chosen.
The term of membership shall be three years, renewable. If a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس ادارة</orig> cannot be elected by the specified date, the existing Board shall continue to manage the company's affairs until the reasons cease to exist and a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> is elected.
The company may have a Chief Executive Officer <orig>رئيسا تنفيذيا</orig> appointed by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> from among its members or others, entrusted with the management of the company. The Board shall determine his allowances and powers to sign on behalf of the company.
Second: Addition of a new Article No. (55) to the company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>, as follows:
The company may buy or sell its shares (treasury shares <orig>أسهم الخزينة</orig>) at their market value, not exceeding 10% of its issued shares, in accordance with Law No. 7/2010 <orig>القانون 2010/7</orig> and its executive regulations and amendments, and in accordance with the controls of the competent regulatory authorities.
<page_end>18</page_end>

# Al-Muzaini Exchange Company <orig>شركة المزيني للصيرفة</orig> (K.S.C.) Closed
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
### Held on Sunday, 16 February 2025

On Sunday, 17 Sha'ban 1446 AH, corresponding to 16 February 2025, at 11:00 AM, the Extraordinary General Assembly met in the meeting room, second floor, at the headquarters of Al-Muzaini Exchange Company <orig>شركة المزيني للصيرفة</orig>. Mr. Mohammed Al-Waqian <orig>محمد الوقيان</orig> attended, representing Gulf Custody Company <orig>الشركة الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig> via Zoom application, and confirmed the completion of the legal quorum for the validity of the meeting, with an attendance rate of 92.37863% (3.6331% shares in person, 88.7455% shares by proxy).
Mr. Abdul Latif Abdul Aziz Yousef Al-Muzaini <orig>عبداللطيف عبدالعزيز يوسف المزيني</orig> attended the meeting – on his own behalf – and in his capacity as Chairman of the Board of Directors, and as a proxy for some shareholders.

## Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
### Announcement
Further to the announcement published in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) No. 1698 dated 4/8/2024, in which an announcement was directed to the esteemed owners of abandoned vessels and marine craft on Ashairej Coast <orig>ساحل عشيرج</orig>, regarding the necessity of visiting the administration's headquarters located in Al-Ardiya Industrial Area <orig>منطقة العارضية الصناعية</orig> – General Directorate of Coast Guard <orig>الإدارة العامة لخفر السواحل</orig> building (former Police Union building) – behind the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>مؤسسة التأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> – next to the Arab Open University <orig>الجامعة العربية المفتوحة</orig>, within a period not exceeding one month from the date of publication of the announcement in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), to update the data of the abandoned and neglected vessels and marine craft on Ashairej Coast <orig>ساحل عشيرج</orig>, along with stating their current condition and contact information of their owners, bringing with them all original documents and papers or official copies thereof proving ownership of these vessels and marine craft.
Therefore, the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> urges all esteemed owners of the marine craft described below not to delay in visiting the administration within the specified period in the announcement, as all legal measures will be taken against their owners, obliging them to bear all expenses resulting from the removal of the vessels and marine craft in accordance with the provisions of Maritime Commercial Law No. 28 of 1980 and Public Authority for Environment Law No. 42 of 2014 and its amendments, and all regulating laws and regulations.

### Description of Item No. (1)
Coordinates: N29 23.215 – E 47 49.870
Location: Ashairej Coast <orig>ساحل عشيرج</orig>
A tugboat type vessel, approximate length 24 meters and approximate width 4.9 meters, with a winch and many ropes at the back. No data is present on it. There is a white-painted cabin with 8 windows and 2 doors. The hull is completely dilapidated and is considered a pile of scrap iron. A blue-painted chimney is visible on it.

### Description of Item No. (2)
Coordinates: N 29 23 21.8 – E 047 49 41.7
Location: Ashairej Coast <orig>ساحل عشيرج</orig>
A fishing vessel, black and white in color, with an iron hull. The stern of the vessel is white and the tower is blue. On top of the tower, there is a black frame, and the tower has a circular mark in the shape of the letter S in the middle, in red with a white background. The cabin consists of two floors, and the letters ALMADIES are present on the hull of the vessel.

### Description of Item No. (3)

11. Garbage collection services. (381101)
12. Sale of environmental pollution control equipment. (477329)
13. Ownership of contracting and real estate for the benefit of the company. (681091)
14. Investing financial surpluses in financial portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities. (649918)
At the end of the meeting, the Chairman thanked the attendees and concluded the Ordinary General Assembly meeting at 12:00 PM on the same day.
Chairman of the Board of Directors

## Med Cell Medical Company K.S.C.C. <orig>شركة ميد سيل الطبية ش.م.ك.م</orig>
### Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
The Extraordinary General Assembly of Med Cell Medical Company K.S.C.C. <orig>شركة ميد سيل الطبية ش.م.ك.م</orig> held its meeting at 11:00 AM on Thursday, 13/02/2025, at Al-Mazaya Tower (1) <orig>برج المزايا</orig>, 19th Floor – Al-Mirqab Area <orig>منطقة المرقاب</orig> – Plot (2) – Khalid Bin Al-Waleed Street <orig>شارع خالد بن الوليد</orig>.
**Attendees:**
1 – Mr. Abdullah Abdullah Ra'ees Al-Rashidi <orig>عبد الله عبد الله رئيس الرشيدي</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors
2 – Shareholders holding 15,000,000 shares, representing 100% of the company's total shares of 15,000,000 shares.
Mr. Abdullah Abdullah Ra'ees Al-Rashidi <orig>عبد الله عبد الله رئيس الرشيدي</orig> opened the meeting in his capacity as Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chairman of the Assembly, welcoming the attendees. After the legal quorum for the Extraordinary General Assembly was met and announced, he proceeded to present and discuss the items on the agenda as follows:
**Item One: Approval was granted to amend Article (6) of the Articles of Incorporation and Article (4) of the Company's Articles of Association:**
**Current Text:**
Without prejudice to the provisions of Decree-Law on Companies No. 1 of 2016 and its amendments and executive regulations, the purposes for which the company was established are "medical purposes" and are as follows:
- 1- Establishment and management of hospitals, medical centers, specialized laboratories, and pharmacies.
- 2- Provision of home medical services.
- 3- Contracting with doctors, patients, and technicians to work for the company and for third parties, whether from outside or inside the country.
- 4- Provision of all types of medical services to governmental and private institutions according to contracts concluded with them.
- 5- Establishment of specialized technical workshops.
- 6- Pharmaceutical manufacturing (subject to the approval of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>).
- 7- Ownership of contracting necessary to carry out its activities within the limits permitted by law.
- 8- Utilizing the company's available financial surpluses by investing them in financial portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities.
The company may carry out the aforementioned activities in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> and abroad, either directly or by agency. The company may also engage in similar, complementary, necessary, or related activities to its stated purposes.
**Text After Amendment:**
Without prejudice to the provisions of Decree-Law on Companies No. 1 of 2016 and its amendments and executive regulations, the purposes for which the company was established are "medical purposes" and are as follows:
- 1- Establishment, operation, and management of private medical centers – Code No. 861043
- 2- Establishment, operation, and management of a private medical laboratory – Code No. 861044
- 3- Establishment, operation, and management of private medical hospitals – Code No. 861047
- 4- Establishment, operation, and management of a private health clinic – Code No. 861049

Companies wishing to participate in the practice must adhere to the following:
1. Submission of a copy of the registration card with the Ministry of Defense / Local Procurement Department <orig>إدارة التجهيز المحلي</orig> for the year 2025.
2. Submission of an authorization letter from the company to purchase the documents.
3. The company must specialize in this field and be classified by the Companies Classification Control <orig>مراقبة تصنيف الشركات</orig> at the Ministry.
4. Submission of a copy of the annual national labor support certificate for non-governmental companies.
5. Submission of an official letter for any inquiries within (one week) from the date of publication of the announcement.
6. Payment of the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents via (K.NET).

Practice No.: 2411-14-16150240
For the Supply of Fire-Fighting Equipment

The Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> announces the issuance of the above-mentioned practice to specialized companies for the year 2025, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Local Procurement Department <orig>إدارة التجهيز المحلي</orig> – Technical Equipment Control <orig>مراقبة التجهيزات الفنية</orig> – during official working hours. # Public Prosecution / Al-Niyaba Al-Amma <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>

*   The Disciplinary Board for Lawyers decided at its session held on 15/12/2024
*   in Case No. 2024/75, Lawyers' Complaints.
*   against / Amal Habib Abbas Boland <orig>أمل حبيب عباس بولند</orig> - Lawyer - Kuwaiti nationality
*   for the charge of :-
    Breaching the provisions of the Lawyers' Profession Law and its duties.
*   a decision stipulating :-
    Acquittal of the accused from the disciplinary violation attributed to her.
    And at the session on 17/2/2025, the Court of Appeal issued a disciplinary decision stipulating:
    Acceptance of the Public Prosecution's appeal formally and substantively by annulling the appealed decision and ruling anew
    to punish the accused by suspension for one month and publication.
    The Public Prosecution announces this judgment by publication in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in accordance with the text of
    Article 41 of Law No. 42 of 1964 regarding the regulation of the legal profession before
    the Courts.

Director of Criminal Enforcement Prosecution

# Ministry of Justice / Wizarat Al-Adl <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>

3:30 PM.

### Announcement of Public Auction for Vehicles
The General Department of Execution <orig>الإدارة العامة للتنفيذ</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 5 March 2025, and the following days, Tuesday and Thursday, starting from 8:00 AM, the following vehicles will be sold by public auction at Al-Doha <orig>الدوحة</orig> impoundment garage, in execution of several judgments. # Seizure Sale Announcement Report

The Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> – Enforcement Directorate <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig>, Compulsory Enforcement Department <orig>قسم التنفيذ الجبري</orig>, Mubarak Al-Kabeer Governorate <orig>محافظة مبارك الكبير</orig> announces that on Tuesday, 8/4/2025, starting from 9:00 AM, movable assets belonging to the government/ Al-Saqr Industries Company <orig>شركة صناعات الصقر</orig> – Hamad Saqr Al-Saqr <orig>حمد صقر الصقر</orig> and Partners, will be sold by public auction at the Sabeehan Industrial Area <orig>صبيحان الصناعية</orig> – Plot (8) – Street (103) – Parcel (172).
These assets are detailed in the executive seizure report dated 16/2/2022, which was seized in favor of/ Industrial Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الصناعي</orig>, in execution of the judgment filed under enforcement file no. 193381580 for an amount of 745.300 K.D. (only seven hundred forty-five thousand three hundred Kuwaiti Dinars).
If this day is not sufficient to complete the sale, it will be completed on the following three days. Therefore, those wishing to purchase must attend at the time and place specified above. For more information, the Compulsory Enforcement Department <orig>قسم التنفيذ الجبري</orig> in Mubarak Al-Kabeer Governorate <orig>محافظة مبارك الكبير</orig> can be consulted during official working hours, and for clarification, we announce.

Head of Enforcement Directorate <orig>إدارة تنفيذ</orig>, Mubarak Al-Kabeer Governorate <orig>محافظة مبارك الكبير</orig>

The Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> – Capital Enforcement Directorate <orig>إدارة تنفيذ العاصمة</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 5/3/

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
28
</header>

As stated in the Municipality's letter, the property is unregulated and construction is not permitted on it except after its regulation or the submission of a subdivision project approved by the Municipality, and the State's right to deduct the percentage that accrues to the State without compensation from the entire area of the original property shall be preserved.

## Secondly: Auction Conditions:

### Firstly:
The auction shall commence at the basic price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.

### Secondly:
Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit, at the time of the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.

### Thirdly:
If the bidder whose bid was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.

### Fourthly:
If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price in that session. Otherwise, the auction shall be awarded in the session based on the price at which the bidder had previously been awarded, with the bidding immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. No bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.

### Sixthly:
In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the expenses of enforcement procedures amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.

### Seventhly:
This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.

### Eighthly:
The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been dispossessed is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

President of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Sale of Shares in a Property by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 24 March 2025, in Hall 48, on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuits No. 163, 165, 167 /2022 Sales/1, filed by:

Property Description (for the sale of the shares of the first and second defendants - Sheikha / Fadia and the share of ):
Property Document No. 2011/8363 located in Al-Shaab <orig>الشعب</orig> area, Plot No. 1, Block No. 8, which is estimated at 17.1354% for each of them, undivided, from its total area (257.02 m²), by public auction with a basic price of 26,331,804 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Twenty-six million, three hundred thirty-one thousand, eight hundred and four Kuwaiti Dinars) for each share separately in the property.
*** According to the attached description certificate dated 2/12/2023.

## Announcement of Public Auction for Real Estate

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Monday, 24/3/2025, in Hall 48, second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2023/284 Sales/1, filed by:
Badriyah Faleh Saif Abu Rdan Al-Azmi <orig>بدريه فالح سيف أبو ردن العازمي</orig>.
Against:
1- Khalid Ali Mohammed Al-Khatlan <orig>خالد على محمد الختلان</orig>.
2- Talal Mohammed Sharar Al-Khatlan <orig>طلال محمد شرار الختلان</orig>.
3- Kuwait Finance House <orig>بيت التمويل الكويتي</orig>.
4- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.

### Property Description (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

**Property No. 1:**
- Property document No. 3783, located in Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area - Plot No. 8 - Block No. 2 - Plan M / 19714, with an area of 1338 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 5,700,000 (Five Million Seven Hundred Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the Description Certificate:
- After inspecting the property, it was found to be commercial, consisting of a ground floor + mezzanine + first floor + second floor + roof. Violations include: creating 5 shops on the ground floor instead of two shops; creating a shop at the property entrance leading to the mezzanine floor using light materials; canceling the mezzanine floor and installing a closed door; expanding the loft <orig>سندرة</orig> of all shops; creating an iron staircase from the mezzanine to the second floor; canceling all light wells <orig>مناور</orig> in the property; and opening some shops into each other.
** According to the Expert's Report
On 30/9/2019, the expert <orig>الخبرة</orig> visited the property subject of the lawsuit, located in Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area, Block (2), Salem Al-Mubarak <orig>سالم المبارك</orig> Street, Plot (8). The building's commercial name is Salmiya Market <orig>سوق السالمية</orig>. The plaintiff's agent was present and provided guidance. The defendants failed to appear despite being properly notified. Mr. Expert of Knowledge <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> was present. The inspection was conducted as follows:
The property conforms to the general and specific specifications of document No. 3783 and has an area of 1338 square meters.
. The property subject of the lawsuit is a commercial complex located on three streets, with two entrances and an external staircase to the first and second floors. There is no elevator. It consists of a ground floor, a loft <orig>سندره</orig>, a first floor, and a second floor. The building is old.
. The ground floor is fully leased to two shops.

Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid one-tenth, the auction shall be immediately re-held at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. No bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied by a full deposit of its value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are requested to proceed at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges having inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Chief Justice of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 24 March 2025, in Hall 48, on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 1/2023/302 Sales/1.

Filed by:
- Issa Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>عيسى صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
- Shaili Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>شيلي صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
- Khulaif Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>خليف صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
- Shukriya Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>شكريه صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
- Houriya Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>حوريه صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
Fawziya Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>فوزيه صحن فهد العنزي</orig>. On their own behalf and in their capacity as heirs of / Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>صحن فهد العنزي</orig>

Against:
1- The Public Authority for Minors' Affairs <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون القصر</orig> in its capacity as guardian of Mr. Khalifa Sahin Fahad Al-Enezi <orig>خليفه صحن فهد العنزي</orig>.
2- The Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> in his capacity.
3- The Director of the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig> in his capacity.

Property Description (According to the attached Description Certificate)
- Property Document No. 1993/6087, located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - Plot No. 238 - Block No. 5 - Plan M / 36874, with an area of 2301, by public auction with a base price of 220,000 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Two Hundred and Twenty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the Description Certificate:
The property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor + first floor + roof, and there are no violations.
** According to the Description Certificate:
On 15/2/2023, we moved to Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - Block (5) - Street (1) - Plot (238) - House (5) - and the automated number (12845553), to inspect the disputed property on site, in the presence and guidance of the first plaintiff and Mr. Sa'ad Mubarak Al-Mutairi <orig>سعد مبارك المطيري</orig>, the expert of knowledge at the department. The inspection was carried out as follows:
The disputed property is a government house consisting of a ground floor and a first floor, located on a single street, externally clad with limestone, and has an area of (301) m2. The disputed property contains two entrances, an entrance for the annex and an entrance for the house. The ground floor consists of two halls, a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>, two rooms, two bathrooms, a kitchen, a room, and a bathroom. The first floor consists of (5) rooms, a hall, a kitchen, two bathrooms, and (3) toilets. The roof consists of a laundry room, two rooms, and a large ceiling. The disputed property does not contain an elevator, and its air conditioning consists of units, a central water heater part, and other normal parts.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction shall be re-held at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was awarded.

## Description of the Third Property: (According to the attached property description certificate)
Property Document No. 2011/1556, located in Al-Fintas <orig>الفنطاس</orig> area - Plot No. 156 - North Expansion <orig>التوسعة الشمالية</orig> Block No. - Plan M / 31564, with an area of 972 m2, to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 1,300,000 (One Million Three Hundred Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
**The property was found to have violations, which are:**
- 1- The owner opened the basement and merged it with the adjacent plot.
- 2- Unlicensed sections were made in the basement.
- 3- A room with an area of 20 m2 was built on the ground floor.
- The disputed property, located in Al-Fintas <orig>الفنطاس</orig> area - Document No. 2011/1556 - Plot No. 156 - North Expansion <orig>التوسعة الشمالية</orig> Block No. - Plan M / 31564, with an area of 972 m2,
- The disputed property is an investment building consisting of a basement, a ground floor, 6 repeated floors, and a roof, with a total area of 972 square meters, clad in beige stone. It is located on one street, bordered by a neighbor on one side, and on the other two sides, there is an independent area for parking.
- The air conditioning in the disputed property is central, and there are 2 elevators.
- The ground floor contains a guard's room with its bathroom, in addition to an annex consisting of two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen. There is also a commercial salon, Roxy Men's Salon <orig>صالون روكسي للرجال</orig>.
- The basement is fully leased to a health club under the trade name Connex Club <orig>نادي كونكس</orig>.
- The first to fifth floors each consist of 7 apartments, which we were unable to inspect from the inside as they are all leased. The guard stated that they are similar and contain two bedrooms, two bathrooms, a living room, and a kitchen.
- The sixth floor consists of 5 apartments, which we were unable to inspect from the inside, and there is no construction on the roof.

## Description of the Fourth Property: (According to the attached property description certificate)
Property Document No. 2018/2074, located in Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area - Plot No. 8 currently and formerly 19 - Block No. 73 formerly and currently 1 - Plan M / 33917, with an area of 1047 m2, to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 1,650,000 (One Million Six Hundred Fifty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
**The property was found to have violations, which are:**
- 1- There is a telecommunications tower on the roof.
- 2- An emergency staircase was not implemented on the roof.
- 3- There is no plan for the 11th floor.
- 4- The basement plan is non-compliant.
- 5- Aluminum glass breakage and closure with light materials.
- 6- Merger of the distributor <orig>الموزع</orig> on floors 10-9-8.
- 7- Construction of an electrical transformer room on the ground floor or cancellation of some ground floor parking spaces.
- 8- There is an expansion in the staircase and the electrical room.
- 9- There is an elevation on the ground floor, which led to the cancellation of some parking spaces.
- 10- Flowerbeds were not implemented.
- 11- There are air conditioning bases.
The disputed property, located in Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area - Document No. 2018/2074 - Plot No. 8 currently and formerly 19 - Block No. 73 formerly and currently 1 - Plan M / 33917, with an area of 1047 m2. The disputed property is an investment building located on two streets (front and back), with an area of 1047 square meters, bordered by neighbors on two sides, and facing a mosque and a shaded parking area. The disputed property consists of a basement, a ground floor, and 11 floors, clad with cinema and stone, and labeled as Property No. 19. The air conditioning in the disputed property is central, and there are 2 elevators. The basement consists of a swimming pool and a room containing bathrooms, showers, and an empty space. The ground floor consists of an outdoor swimming pool, reception, and lobby. The 11th floor consists of a health club, entertainment games (billiards), and a lounge. Floors 1 to 4 consist of 6 apartments on each floor, while floors 5 to 10 contain 5 apartments on each floor, which we were unable to inspect from the inside.

1- Hassan Abdulredha Abdulkarim Abdulkarim <orig>حسن عبدالرضا عبدالكريم عبدالكريم</orig>.

19- Hussein Abdulredha Abdulkarim <orig>حسين عبدالرضا عبدالكريم</orig>.
against Sayyid Abbas Al-Mousawi <orig>سيد عباس الموسوي</orig> in his capacity as supervisor <orig>ناظر</orig> of Waqf <orig>وقفية</orig> No. 1996/45 and Waqf <orig>وقف</orig> Deed No. 1998/83, and added to inheritance inventory <orig>حصر الوراثة</orig> No. 219 dated 22/6/2005.

Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate <orig>شهادة الأوصاف</orig>)
Property of Document No. 1974/4102 located in Al-Jabriya <orig>الجابرية</orig> area – Plot No. 66 – Block No. 1 – Plan M/33254 currently – and previously/25969, with an area of 750 m2, by public auction <orig>المزاد العلني</orig> at a base price of K.D. 480,000 (Four Hundred Eighty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
**
According to the description certificate <orig>شهادة الأوصاف</orig>:
- After inspecting the property based on the plans attached to the technical file, it was found to be a private residence consisting of a ground floor + first floor + second floor + annex. The text of the plans and registration fees indicated that it does not conform to the plans, and there are violations, namely an increase in construction on the ground floor, first floor, and second floor. There are annexes not included in the license, and the balcony on the second floor has been enclosed with light materials.
**
According to the expert's report <orig>تقرير الخبير</orig>:
- The property in dispute conforms in terms of general and specific specifications to real estate document No. 1974/4102, with an area of 750 m2.
- The disputed property is a private residential house overlooking one street and serving neighbors from three sides, with a courtyard <orig>حوش</orig> of 22x5 m2.
- The property in dispute consists of a ground floor, first floor, and second floor, externally clad with mosaic, and has (3) main exits – a side exit for the annexes – and a side exit for the tenants of the first and second floors.
- The plaintiff guided on the components of the property according to the submitted plan, which are detailed as follows:
The ground floor consists of:
- (4) rooms – (4) bathrooms – (1) living room – (1) kitchen + maid's room + (7) rented annexes.
Each annex contains:
- (1) bedroom – (1) bathroom – (1) kitchen with an area of (53) m2 for each annex.
The type of air conditioning in all annexes is (units).
The first floor consists of:
- (4) rooms – (2) bathrooms – (1) living room – (1) kitchen – maid's room with its bathroom – storage room.
The second floor consists of:
- (4) rooms – (2) bathrooms – (1) living room – (1) kitchen – maid's room with its bathroom – storage room.
The side entrance to the disputed property is a large courtyard <orig>حوش</orig> with an area of (15x7) m2.
The type of air conditioning is (central), and there is no elevator.
Second: Auction Conditions <orig>شروط المزاد</orig>:
First: The auction shall start at the base price, and participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, at the time of the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit one-fifth of the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless a new bid is submitted by:
a- Ittijah Gholoum Ali Ashkanani <orig>اتجاه غلوم علي اشكناني</orig> on her own behalf and as guardian <orig>الولي</orig> of her minor daughters, namely:
1- Sakina Mohammed Abdulredha Abdulkarim <orig>سكينة محمد عبدالرضا عبدالكريم</orig>.
2- Fajr Mohammed Abdulredha Abdulkarim <orig>فجر محمد عبدالرضا عبدالكريم</orig>.
3- Mohsen Mohammed Abdulredha Abdulkarim <orig>محسن محمد عبدالرضا عبدالكريم</orig>.
4- Abdulredha Mohammed Abdulredha <orig>عبدالرضا محمد عبدالرضا</orig>.
b- Nasser Mohammed Abdulkarim Abdulredha <orig>ناصر محمد عبدالكريم عبدالرضا</orig>.
c- Yaqoub Mohammed Abdulkarim Abdulredha <orig>يعقوب محمد عبدالكريم عبدالرضا</orig>.
d- Kawthar Mohammed Abdulkarim Abdulredha <orig>كوثر محمد عبدالكريم عبدالرضا</orig>.
e- Kafiya Jawad Ahmed Mohammed <orig>كافيه جواد أحمد محمد</orig> on her own behalf and as guardian <orig>الولي</orig> of her minor sons, namely:
1- Abdulredha Mohammed Abdulredha <orig>عبدالرضا محمد عبدالرضا</orig>.
2- Fajr Mohammed Abdulredha <orig>فجر محمد عبدالرضا</orig>.

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2/3/2025 AD
33
