Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to increase the bid by one-tenth, the auction shall be immediately re-held at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid unaccompanied by a full deposit of its value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transferring and registering ownership, the expenses of enforcement procedures amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and is requested by those directly involved in the sale procedures, at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges having inspected the property with an inspection that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

### Criminal Judgment Announcement

The Misdemeanor Court <orig>محكمة الجنح</orig>, in its session held on 2021-02-21,
in Case No.: 001292 / 20 – Commercial Affairs Prosecution <orig>نيابة شئون تجاري</orig> - Misdemeanors, Checks,
Police Station No.: (000016 / 20 – Jleeb Al-Shuyoukh <orig>جليب الشيوخ</orig>) –
Automated Case No.: 201535640
Against the accused: Ayman Yousef Hussein Al-Amir <orig>أيمن يوسف حسين الأمير</orig>
Nationality: Egypt
Civil ID No.: 270011903133
issued a default judgment <orig>حكماً غيابياً</orig> sentencing: the accused to one year imprisonment with labor and enforcement for the charge attributed to him.
And ordered his deportation from the country after serving his sentence.
Referred the civil claim to the competent court, and instructed the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة كتاب</orig> of this General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> to set a session for its consideration, notify the parties, and reserved judgment on the expenses.
The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to enforce it in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>, noting that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the second day of publication, passes without the convicted person appealing by objection or appeal, the judgment becomes final and enforceable against them.
Director of Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

## Organization and Objection Committee <orig>لجنة التنظيم والاعتراض</orig>
### Decisions Issued by the Organization and Objection Committee <orig>لجنة التنظيم والاعتراض</orig>
### In Cases of Lineage and Name Correction
The Committee, at its meeting No. (4) dated 18/2/2025, issued (3) decisions
in the following files:
1- In Organization No. (2024/169) related to Application No. (2024/2073)
submitted by/ Adel Ali Sulaiman Al-Abd Al-Sharqi <orig>عادل علي سليمان العبد الشرقي</orig>, approving the deletion of the surname
(Al-Sharqi) and the addition of the surname (Al-Sharqi) so that the full name becomes / Adel Ali Sulaiman Al-Abd
Al-Sharqi <orig>عادل علي سليمان العبد الشرقي</orig>. This applies to all official documents for him, his siblings (Ahmed <orig>أحمد</orig>, Ruqayya <orig>رقيه</orig>), their children,
and grandchildren, based on the submitted papers.
2- In Organization No. (2024/170) related to Application No. (2023/1505)
submitted by/ Ahmed Shaker Rahim Nina Jani <orig>أحمد شاكر رحيم نينا جاني</orig>, approving the amendment of the name from /
Shoto Shankar Rad Sinaya <orig>شوتو شنكر راد سينايا</orig> to / Ahmed Shaker Rahim Nina Jani <orig>أحمد شاكر رحيم نينا جاني</orig>, in his birth certificate,
and in all official documents for him, his siblings (Amira <orig>أميره</orig>, Sabeeha <orig>سبيحه</orig>), their children, and the children of his deceased brother
(Abdul Amir <orig>عبد الأمير</orig>), based on the submitted papers.
3- In Organization No. (2025/4) related to Application No. (2024/1182) submitted by/ Jassim
Mustafa Abdul Rasool Mohammed Ahmed <orig>جاسم مصطفى عبد الرسول محمد أحمد</orig>, approving the addition of the grandfather's name (Shafi' <orig>شفیع</orig>) and the addition
of the surname (Kayhani <orig>كيهاني</orig>) so that the full name becomes / Jassim Mustafa Abdul Rasool Mohammed Shafi' Ahmed Kayhani <orig>جاسم مصطفى عبد الرسول محمد شفیع أحمد كيهاني</orig>.
This applies to all official documents for him, his siblings (Maryam <orig>مريم</orig>, Wadha <orig>وضحا</orig>), their children, and the children of his deceased brother
(Abdul Amir <orig>عبد الأمير</orig>), based on the submitted papers.

## Announcement of a Criminal Judgment
Mubarak Al-Kabeer Court <orig>محكمة مبارك الكبير</orig>, at its sessions held on 21-02-2021, issued:
In Case No.: 000878 / 20 – Commercial Affairs Prosecution, Network Misdemeanors
Police Station No.: 0000163 / 20 – (Al-Sharq <orig>الشرق</orig>) –
Automated Case No.: 201045700
Against the accused: Mo'taz Mohammed Jameel Ma'sarani <orig>معتز محمد جميل معصراني</orig>
Nationality: Syrian
Civil ID No.: 282032505394
An in absentia judgment ruling: –
Imprisoning the accused for six months with labor and enforcement for the charge attributed to him, and ordered his deportation
from the country after the execution of his sentence. The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment
and instructs all security authorities to enforce it in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedures
and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the second day of
publication, elapses without the convicted person appealing by objection or appeal, the judgment becomes final
and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>مدير نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

## Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>
### Announcement of Sealed Bid Auction
Auction No. (2449)

The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of aluminum scrap - computers - iron and helium scrap - telephones and fax machines - various electrical appliances that are out of use, by sealed bid auction at Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, according to the following details:
1- Location for receiving the terms and conditions booklet and submitting participation in the auction: Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> - Financial Affairs Department, from 2 March 2025 to 6 March 2025. Documents will be handed over for a non-refundable fee of (30) Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> payable at Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>.
The bidder will sign a declaration and undertaking at the time of receiving the terms and conditions booklet to adhere to the specified deadline for submitting the offer to the Central Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع المركزي</orig> at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
2- Inspection Date: (5) working days from 2 March 2025 to 6 March 2025. Inspection Time: During official working hours (from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM).
3- Location for receiving those wishing to inspect: General Warehouses Department in Shuwaikh Industrial Area <orig>منطقة الشويخ الصناعية</orig>.
4- Date for submitting offers and opening envelopes:
*   Submission of offers on Sunday, 9 March 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Storage Affairs Department - Central Sales Section for the auction specified for bidders by Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> (no offer will be accepted after the bidder's specified deadline).
*   Opening of envelopes and holding of the auction on Monday, 10 March 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Storage Affairs Department.
*   Announcement of the successful bidder on the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> website on Monday, 10 March 2025.
*   Delivery of checks to unsuccessful bidders on Tuesday, 11 March 2025.
*   The certified check must be submitted in the name of Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>.
Special Conditions:
*   The bidder must be Kuwaiti - an individual or a Kuwaiti company - registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. A foreigner may participate provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or commercial agent with a notarized contract. (Must attach: copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, copy of the company license, copy of the civil ID, and an authorized power of attorney from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all valid).
*   Kuwaiti individuals are allowed to participate in the auction (must attach a copy of the civil ID).
*   Bidders must attach a certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage issued by the Ministry of Social Affairs and Labor <orig>وزارة الشؤون الاجتماعية والعمل</orig> before signing the contract, in accordance with Article (6) of Law No. (19 of 2000) and the decision of the Central Tenders Committee <orig>لجنة المناقصات المركزية</orig> in this regard, along with copies of supporting documents.
*   To receive the terms and conditions booklet: Please contact Mr. Mahdi Al-Nahw <orig>مهدي النحو</orig>, Tel: 60959163
*   Inspection site official: Please contact Mr. Ahmed Al-Rashidi <orig>احمد الرشيدي</orig>, Tel: 51455595

### Announcement of Sealed Bid Auction
Auction No. (2450) and Auction No. (2451)

The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of computers and their accessories - metal and wooden furniture - iron and aluminum scrap - telephones and fax machines - various electrical appliances, and (80) vehicles (Group One), comprising 76 partially damaged and 4 totally damaged, that are out of use, by sealed bid auction at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>, according to the following details:
1- Location for receiving the terms and conditions booklet and submitting participation in both auctions:
*   Auction No. (2450): Sale document for computers and their accessories - metal and wooden furniture - iron and aluminum scrap - telephones and fax machines - various electrical appliances (Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> - General Department of Logistics <orig>الإدارة العامة للإمداد</orig> "Warehouses Department" Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig>)
*   Auction No. (2451): Sale document for (80) vehicles (Group One), comprising 76 partially damaged and 4 totally damaged (Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> - General Department of Logistics <orig>الإدارة العامة للإمداد</orig> "Vehicles Department" Subhan <orig>صبحان</orig>)
The bidder will sign a declaration and undertaking at the time of receiving the terms and conditions booklet to adhere to the specified deadline for submitting the offer to the Central Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع المركزي</orig> at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.

3- Location for receiving those wishing to inspect for bidders:
*   Auction No. (2450): - Former Special Forces (Sixth Ring Road) - Mina Abdullah <orig>ميناء عبدالله</orig> - Al-Naeem <orig>النعيم</orig>
*   Auction No. (2451): Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> - Mina Abdullah <orig>ميناء عبدالله</orig> Scrap Yard.
4- Date for submitting offers and opening envelopes:
*   Submission of offers on Tuesday, 11 March 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Storage Affairs Department - Central Sales Section for the auction specified for the bidder by Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> (no offer will be accepted after the bidder's specified deadline).
*   Opening of envelopes and holding of the auction on Wednesday, 12 March 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Storage Affairs Department.

*   Delivery of checks to unsuccessful bidders on Thursday, 13 March 2025.
*   Certified checks / bank guarantee must be submitted in the name of the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
Special Conditions for Bidders:

A foreigner may participate provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or commercial agent with a notarized contract. (Must attach: copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, copy of the company license, copy of the civil ID, and an authorized power of attorney from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all valid).
*   Special conditions for Auction No. (2450): (No civil ID copy required).
*   Special conditions for Auction No. (2451):
*   The successful bidder for the scrap car auction shall, at their own expense, remove the original color of the vehicles completely at their location and before any procedures for their removal or transfer of ownership.

# Public Authority for Agriculture and Fish Resources <orig>الهيئة العامة لشؤون الزراعة والثروة السمكية</orig>

The Authority announces the offering of Tender No. H/M/Z/1-2025/2024 for the exploitation of the Zoo Restaurant building, Plot 2. Companies and establishments wishing to participate in this tender can obtain the tender document by submitting a letter expressing their desire to purchase the tender, accompanied by authorization from the signatory of the company or establishment, during official working hours from the Financial Affairs Department (Tenders Section) at the Authority's main headquarters – Al-Rabiya <orig>الرابية</orig> – Al-Ghazali Street <orig>شارع الغزالي</orig>.

- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM at the Authority's headquarters.
- The aforementioned cash payment must be made by certified check or K-Net card.
- The deadline for submitting any reservations or inquiries regarding the aforementioned tender is one week after the announcement date, and no attention will be paid to such requests after this date.
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.

- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the bid format and initial insurance, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session.
- Interested companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the relevant department before the specified date for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1- Copy of the Civil ID.
2- Copy of the authorized signature.
3- In case of attendance by a person other than the authorized signatory, a written letter of authorization from the authorized signatory must be presented, delegating whomever they deem fit to attend the session.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from the fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Clause (13) of Circular No. 2023/1 regarding tenders in public entities.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the tender must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.

It also features a detailed announcement for a tender to purchase a PhotoFinish camera system for the Kuwait Camel Racing Club."

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
41
</header>

- All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-reproducible hard copy, except for the tender form and the preliminary bond, which must be submitted as a hard copy. Tenders shall be valid for (90) ninety days from the date of opening the tenders. Any tender not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the preliminary guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
- The tenderer must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Please note that any tender not including this certificate will be excluded.
- The tenderer must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.
The practice is open to all companies and establishments specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025. A non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, payable via K-Net, is required (refundable only in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars). Applicants must bring the following:
1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette.
2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
3- A written letter of authorized delegation with the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> – a copy of the signature authorization).
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise. This is in accordance with the text of Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016, which states: "Tender envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session attended by the tenderers or their representatives."
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as companies wishing to attend the envelope opening session have the right to coordinate with the competent committee before the session date.
- This announcement is considered an integral part of the practice documents.
Note: The Authority may cancel the practice without stating reasons and without any objection from the practitioners.
- For more information, please visit the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw)

Acting Deputy Director General for Finance and Administrative Affairs Sector

Announcement
The Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> announces the launch of Practice No. H.A.R.D. 82/2024/2025 concerning the purchase of a photo-finish camera for the finish line (arbitration committee) for the Kuwaiti Camel Racing Club <orig>النادي الكويتي لسباق الهجن</orig>, in sealed envelopes, according to the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents. These documents can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department – Tenders and Practices Section – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

Tenders must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red wax and placed in the designated box for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Second Floor). No tenders received after the specified closing time for the practice will be accepted.
- Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding the submission of tenders (CD) on the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

Acting Deputy Director General for Finance and Administrative Affairs Sector

## Announcement

The Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. A.D. 84 / 2024/2025 concerning the supply and installation of grandstand seats and VIP box seats at Sabah Al-Salem Stadium <orig>استاد صباح السالم</orig> at Al-Arabi Sporting Club <orig>النادي العربي الرياضي</orig>, in sealed envelopes, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents. These documents can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department – Tenders and Practices Section – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

<table_caption>Tender Details and Initial Guarantee</table_caption>
<table>
| Offer Date | Closing Date | Document Price | Initial Guarantee |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 2/3/2025    | 12/3/2025      | 75 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Only (K.D. 1,500) One Thousand Five Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee valid for (90) days in favor of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> from the closing date |
</table>

A preliminary meeting for the practitioners has been scheduled to be held at the Authority's headquarters (First Floor) at 11:00 AM on Thursday, 6 March 2025 AD.

Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the closing date. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red wax and placed in the designated box for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor). No bids received after the specified closing time for the practice will be accepted.

*   Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding bid submission (CD) on the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
*   Companies / practitioners wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must do so at the time and place specified above in the preliminary social schedule (inquiry session). No inquiries will be considered after the deadline.
*   All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-reproducible hard copy, except for the bid form and initial guarantee, which must be submitted as a hard copy. Bids shall be valid for (90) ninety days from the date of bid opening. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the initial guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.

The practice is open to all companies and establishments specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (K.D. 75) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), accompanied by the following:

1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
3- A written letter of authorization approved by the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> – a copy of the signature authorization).

*   Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49 / 2016).
*   Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development and Care <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, indicating their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
*   In accordance with Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49 of 2016 AD), which states: "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session attended by bidders or their representatives."
*   This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as companies wishing to attend the bid opening session have the right to coordinate with the competent committee before the session date.
*   This announcement is considered an integral part of the practice documents.

Note: The Authority reserves the right to cancel the practice without stating reasons and without any objection from the practitioners.

Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
46
</header>
the closing date, provided that bids are submitted in sealed envelopes with red wax, and placed in the box designated for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor). No bids received after the specified deadline for closing the practice will be accepted.
* Bidders must adhere to the instructions for submitting bids (CD) on the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
* Companies / bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, or other matters must do so at the time and place specified in the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). No inquiries will be considered after the deadline.
* All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-copyable hard copy, with the exception of the bid form and initial insurance, which must be submitted as a hard copy. Bids shall remain valid for ninety (90) days from the date of bid opening. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the initial guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
* The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Please note that any bid not including this certificate will be excluded.
* The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> confirming clearance from consumption debts.
The practice is open to all companies and establishments specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars (K.D. 75) only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), accompanied by the following:
1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette.
2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
3- A written letter of authorized delegation to the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID – a copy of the signature authorization).
* Owners of Small and Medium-sized Enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from the fees prescribed for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016.
* Owners of Small and Medium-sized Enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise with the Fund.
In accordance with the text of Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016, which states: "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session attended by bidders or their representatives."
* This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as it is the right of interested companies to coordinate with the designated committee before the day of the session to attend the bid opening session.
* This announcement is considered an integral part of the practice documents.
Note: The Authority may cancel the practice without stating reasons and without any objection from the bidders.
* For more information, please visit the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw).
Deputy Director General for Finance and Administrative Affairs (Acting)

Announcement
The Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> announces Practice No. PAS (2024/2025/91) concerning the supply, installation, maintenance, and warranty of net posts, and the supply and installation of court flooring (Traflex), in accordance with the specifications approved by the International Volleyball Federation <orig>الاتحاد الدولي لكرة الطائرة</orig>, at the Kuwait Volleyball Federation <orig>الاتحاد الكويتي لكرة الطائرة</orig> Hall within the Sheikh Saad Al-Abdullah <orig>الشيخ سعد العبد الله</orig> Sports Complex for Indoor Halls. This is to be done in sealed envelopes according to the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department – Tenders and Practices Section – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

A preliminary meeting for bidders has been scheduled to be held at the Authority's headquarters (First Floor) at 11:00 AM on Tuesday, 4 March 2025 AD.
Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM at the Kuwait Sports Club <orig>نادي الكويت الرياضي</orig>.
This is to be done in sealed envelopes according to the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Services and Suppliers Department – Tenders and Practices Section – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the Public Authority for Sport's <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

Preliminary Meeting
(Inquiry Session) <orig>جلسة استفسارات</orig>
11:00 AM on Wednesday, 2025/03/05, at the
Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (First Floor).
Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the
closing date. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red
wax, and placed in the designated box for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor). No
bids received after the specified closing time for the practice will be accepted.

*   This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as companies wishing to attend the bid opening session have the right to coordinate with the specialized committee before the day of the session.
*   This announcement is an integral part of the practice documents.
*   Note: The Authority may cancel the practice without stating reasons and without any objection from the practitioners.
*   For more information, please visit the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw).

Acting Deputy Director General for Finance and Administrative Affairs Sector <orig>قطاع المالية والإدارية</orig>
Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>

*   Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding bid submission (CD) on the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
*   Companies/practitioners wishing to submit inquiries or clarifications, etc., must do so at the time and place specified above in the Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session) <orig>جلسة استفسارات</orig> schedule. No inquiries will be considered after the deadline.
*   All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-reproducible hard copy, except for the bid form and preliminary insurance, which require a hard copy. Bids are valid for (90) ninety days from the date of bid opening. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the preliminary bond, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning private sector work. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.
*   Practices are open to all companies and establishments specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (K.D. 75) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), accompanied by the following:
    1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
    2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
    3- A written letter of the approved license with the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> - a copy of the signature authorization).
*   Owners of small and medium enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016.
*   Owners of small and medium enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach with their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, including its accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
*   In accordance with the text of Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016, which states: "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session attended by bidders or their representatives."

The Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> announces the extension of the closing period for Tender No. (2-2022/2021), which pertains to securing integrated dynamic management, operating ground handling services, establishing and maintaining facilities, and providing the necessary equipment and provisions.
Please note that the new deadline for submitting bids will be at (1:00 PM) on (Thursday) corresponding to (13/03/2025) instead of (Sunday) corresponding to (02/03/2025). Any bid submitted after this deadline will be rejected.

# Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>
## Announcement

The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> announces its desire to re-tender Practice No. (15-2024/2025) related to the supply of a biometric fingerprint system. Specialized companies wishing to apply for this practice must observe the following:
1.  The company must be registered with the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>.
2.  The applying company must have experience in this field prior to the issuance of this announcement, with proof thereof.
3.  The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms starting from the date of this announcement for a period of 10 days.
4.  The practice terms can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig>.
5.  A preliminary meeting with the bidders will be held on Thursday, 6 March 2025, at 11:00 AM in the building of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الأعلى للتخطيط</orig> – Second Floor.
6.  Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> at the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> no later than 12:00 PM on Thursday, 13 March 2025.

{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Municipality and Central Agency for Public Tenders Announcements",

  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains several official announcements from the Kuwait Municipality and the Central Agency for Public Tenders. It includes notices for cleaning works and car rental tenders, as well as announcements regarding contractor classification release and a tender for exploiting a restaurant site, detailing submission deadlines and requirements."

<header>
51
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH - 2 March 2025 AD
</header>
Based on Article (19) of Municipality Resolution No. (2009/161) regarding the classification, licensing, and registration of building and demolition contractors in Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, which stipulates that a contractor may submit a request to the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> to cancel their registration before its expiry or to cancel the classification, and the committee stipulated in Article One of this regulation may issue its decision to that effect after fulfilling the following two conditions:
1- The contractor has completed all contracted works.
2- Fifteen (15) days have passed from the date of publication of this request in the Official Gazette.
The cancellation of the license or registration shall result in the refund of the bank guarantee submitted by the contractor, taking into account the last paragraph of Article (10) of this resolution.
Accordingly, the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> appeals to anyone who has any claims against the aforementioned contractor regarding construction contracts concluded between them and not yet completed, or judicial reservations in their favor due to violating contracting works or dues arising from the contracting agreement, to review the Contractors Department <orig>قسم المقاولين</orig> at the Engineering Systems Department <orig>إدارة الأنظمة الهندسية</orig> within a maximum period of fifteen days from this date. The Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> will not consider any claims submitted after the prescribed period.

Director General of the Municipality <orig>مدير عام البلدية</orig>

# Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>
## Notice
Regarding Tender No. 2024/16
Cleaning works for mosques and buildings affiliated with the Mosques Department <orig>إدارة مساجد</orig> of Al-Jahra Governorate <orig>محافظة الجهراء</orig> and any other sites in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>
- Ministry of Islamic Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الإسلامية</orig> -
The Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> wishes to draw the attention of the esteemed bidders that the correct closing date for the aforementioned tender is Sunday, 25 May 2025, and not as stated in the announcement published in the Official Gazette Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> on 23 February 2025.
Hence, this notice was necessary.
Secretary General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الأمين العام للجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

## Announcement 2025/23
Regarding the offering of Bid No. 2024/4 for the exploitation of the Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> Center's Paper Gate site (restaurant)
Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> announces the offering of Bid No. 2024/4 for the exploitation of the Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> Center's Paper Gate site (restaurant).
Specialized companies wishing to participate in this bid, which are capable of providing all necessary requirements to perform the requested service at the best possible level of goods and services specific to this license, in accordance with the Municipality's <orig>البلدية</orig> standards regarding external appearance (clothing and cleanliness of workers), arrangement, organization, cleanliness, and quality of food materials provided, must review Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> (Administrative Building, 7th Floor - Tenders and Bids Control <orig>مراقبة المناقصات والمزايدات</orig>) during official working hours to obtain the bid documents for a fee of K.D. 200 (Two Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars only). This amount is non-refundable under any circumstances. Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> approved by the National Fund for SME Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from these fees.
The bidder must inspect the service performance site with an inspection that negates ignorance before the date of the preliminary meeting, to enable bidders to raise their inquiries in the preliminary meeting to achieve the principle of transparency.
The preliminary meeting with bidders who have obtained the bid documents will be held at 10:00 AM on Tuesday, 8 April 2025, at the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> branch building in Al-Ahmadi Governorate <orig>محافظة الأحمدي</orig>. Companies and institutions must submit the receipt of payment for the prescribed fee along with a letter from the company or institution stating their authorization to attend the preliminary meeting.
All companies submitting their bids in the auction must send a representative to attend the technical session for opening the bid envelopes submitted in the auction, scheduled for Monday, 14 April 2025. Please note that in case of non-compliance with attendance, the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> shall not bear any responsibility for that.
Bids must be submitted in sealed envelopes, stamped with red wax, with the bid number and subject written on them, provided that the name of the bidder or anything indicating it is not written on the envelope. They should be placed in the designated box located at Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> (Administrative Building, 7th Floor - Tenders and Bids Control <orig>مراقبة المناقصات والمزايدات</orig>) no later than 12:00 PM on Monday, 14 April 2025, which is the last deadline for accepting bids. An initial security deposit of no less than 2% (two percent) and no more than 5% of the bid value must be deposited with the bid.
If you wish to review the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig>, please make an appointment by accessing the link:
www.baladia.gov.kw

Director General of the Municipality <orig>مدير عام البلدية</orig>

## Announcement

<table>
| No. | Description | Sale Price | Inspection Date | Preliminary Meeting | Closing Date | Initial Security Deposit Percentage |
|:--|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | Re-offering of Auction No. 2024-2024 / 14 for the exploitation and management of rest area No. 4 to provide grocery services – for 5 years – Nutrition Department – Kuwait University <orig>جامعة الكويت</orig> | 75 K.D. | 2025/03/18 10:30 AM | 2025/03/23 11:30 AM Nutrition Department | 2025/04/08 | 2% of the total bid value |
| 2 | Re-offering of Auction No. 2025/2024 / 3 for the exploitation and management of the Central Library, Fifth Floor, to provide light meal services for five years – Nutrition Department – Kuwait University <orig>جامعة الكويت</orig> | 75 K.D. | 2025/03/19 10:30 AM | 2025/03/23 12:00 PM Nutrition Department | 2025/04/08 | 2% of the total bid value |
</table>

Auction documents can be obtained starting from Sunday, 2025/03/02, and on subsequent days during official working hours from the Procurement Department's website ( https://pur.ku.edu.kw ).
2- The final deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, 2025/03/25, at 12:00 PM. Bids received after this time will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session.
3- Bids must be submitted on optical discs (CDs) (3 copies), ensuring that all files have been correctly copied before depositing the discs in the submission envelope. The discs must be identical, similar, protected, non-modifiable, and each must contain all auction documents signed and sealed with the bidder's (company's) stamp.
4- Inquiries will be accepted within 10 days from the announcement date. No inquiries will be accepted after the specified deadline.
5- The following paper documents must be submitted:
- The original copy of the bid form and undertaking.
- Initial security deposit (as per the auction announcement).
- Purchase receipt from the website.
- A copy of the valid national labor percentage certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, indicating no suspension on the bidder's file.
- The envelope designated for the auction.
The bid will be disqualified if any document mentioned in the instructions is not submitted.
6- Bids must be placed in the designated box at the Procurement Department – Sabah Al-Salem University City (Al-Shadadiya) <orig>مدينة صباح السالم الجامعية ( الشدادية )</orig> – Administration Building – Sixth Floor – Suppliers Affairs Section.
Note:
- Auction documents are to be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the University's Suppliers Affairs Section and with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, during official working hours.
- The preliminary meeting will be held at the Nutrition Department – Sabah Al-Salem University City (Al-Shadadiya) <orig>مدينة صباح السالم الجامعية ( الشدادية )</orig> – Administration Building – Sixth Floor.

2- The final deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, 2025/03/25, at 12:00 PM. Bids received after this time will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session.
3- Instructions for Practitioners:
- Bids must be submitted on optical discs (CDs) (3 copies), ensuring that all files have been correctly copied before depositing the discs in the submission envelope. The discs must be identical, similar, protected, non-modifiable, and each must contain all practice documents signed and sealed with the practitioner's (company's) stamp.
- Inquiries will be accepted within 10 days from the announcement date. No inquiries will be accepted after the specified deadline.
- The following paper documents must be submitted:
- The original copy of the bid form and undertaking.
- Initial security deposit (as per the offering announcement).
- Purchase receipt from the website.
- A copy of the valid national labor percentage certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, indicating no suspension on the practitioner's file.
- The envelope designated for the practice.
The bid will be disqualified if any document mentioned in the instructions is not submitted.
1- Bids must be placed in the designated box at the Procurement Department – Sabah Al-Salem University City (Al-Shadadiya) <orig>مدينة صباح السالم الجامعية ( الشدادية )</orig> – Administration Building – Sixth Floor – Suppliers Affairs Section.
Note:
- Practice documents are to be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the University's Suppliers Affairs Section and with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, during official working hours.
<page_end>52</page_end>

53
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1728, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 2 Ramadan 1446 AH – 2 March 2025 AD
Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>
Announcement
</header>
The Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig> announces the submission by:

<table_caption>Competition Protection Agency Announcement Details</table_caption>
<table>
| Activity: Holding Company |
|:---|
| <image_caption>BRF Logo</image_caption> <image> { "description": "BRF logo", "type": "logo", "data": "BRF logo with stylized text" } </image> |
| BRF GmbH <orig>شركة بي ار اف جي ام بي اتش</orig> (Austria) |
</table>

<table_caption>Panda Henan Food Company Details</table_caption>
<table>
| Activity: Production of more processed food products |
|:---|
| <image_caption>OSI Logo</image_caption> <image> { "description": "OSI logo", "type": "logo", "data": "OSI logo with globe design" } </image> |
| Panda Henan Food Company <orig>شركة باندا هيمنان فود</orig>, a subsidiary wholly owned by Henan Best Foods Limited <orig>شركة هيمنان بيست فودز ليمتد</orig> (China) |
</table>

requesting approval for the completion of an economic concentration process through the acquisition by BRF GmbH <orig>شركة بي ار اف جي ام بي اتش</orig> (Austria) of 100% of the capital of Panda Henan Food Company <orig>شركة باندا هيمنان فود</orig>, a subsidiary wholly owned by Henan Best Foods Limited <orig>شركة هيمنان بيست فودز ليمتد</orig>.
In accordance with Law No. (72) of 2020 concerning Competition Protection <orig>حماية المنافسة</orig> and Article (83) of its Executive Regulations issued by Resolution No. (14) of 2021 and its amendments, which stipulate that "any interested party may submit a reasoned objection to the Agency <orig>الجهاز</orig> regarding the economic concentration request within a period not exceeding (15) fifteen days from the date of notification or publication...".
Accordingly, the Agency <orig>الجهاز</orig> invites any interested party to submit their reasoned objection to this economic concentration within a period not exceeding fifteen days from the date of this announcement.
Objection data should be submitted to the headquarters of the Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>, Al-Khadra Tower <orig>برج الخضراء</orig>, 14th Floor, by filling out the form available on the website, along with paying the prescribed fee.

# Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig>
Public Tender Announcement
The Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> announces the issuance of Tender No.: PAHW / M /
1270 – 2024/2025 for the supply, installation, manufacturing, and maintenance of main and sub-transformer stations
with a voltage of
11/132/400 kV <orig>ك. ف</orig>
for the Affordable Housing Project <orig>مشروع المساكن الميسرة</orig>.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Public Authority for Housing Welfare</table_caption>
<table>
| Issue Date | Closing Date | Document Sale Price | Initial Guarantee |
|:------|:-------|:---|:---|
| 2024/03/06 | 2025/04/10 | K.D. 500 | K.D. 500,000 |
| | | | Valid for (90) days |
</table>

Local and international companies executing projects for the supply, installation, implementation, and maintenance of main transformer stations with a voltage of (400/132/11 kV <orig>ك.ف</orig>), or (300/132/11 kV <orig>ك.ف</orig>), and which meet the list of foundations and criteria required from bidders, are invited to purchase the tender documents and submit all required documents and papers in accordance with the requirements, fulfilling the conditions and in the prescribed manner.

First: Tender documents can be obtained from the Documents and Contracts Department <orig>إدارة الوثائق والعقود</orig> – Third Floor – Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> Headquarters – South Surra <orig>جنوب السرة</orig>, in accordance with the following terms and requirements when purchasing the tender documents:
1. For local companies, a registration certificate issued by the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> of the Ministry of Commerce <orig>وزارة التجارة</orig>, a registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>, the company's articles of association, and a company registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> (a recent certificate for the tender year) must be submitted.
2. A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> must be submitted.
3. For international companies, the company's articles of association and a registration certificate issued by the competent authorities in its country of origin must be submitted, provided that they are authenticated by the official authorities in the country of establishment, and attested by a Kuwaiti consulate or any other entity authorized to attest, and translated by an accredited translation office within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, along with a signature authentication letter and a recent registration certificate from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

4. Tender documents shall be handed over against a non-refundable amount as specified in the table above, by certified check issued in favor of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> or K-Net card.
5. A letter of authorization from the company in the name of the person authorized to purchase the tender documents must be submitted, along with a copy of the civil ID of the same authorized person and a signature authentication certificate.
- Please note that the purchase of tender documents will not be permitted unless all the above-mentioned requirements and conditions are met.
6. Companies that have received a valid penalty in state tenders and projects will not be allowed to participate.
7. Companies with ongoing (under execution) contracts that are delayed in delivering any part of the project beyond the contractual completion date by a delay percentage exceeding (50%) of the total contract duration will not be allowed to participate until the contract under execution is settled.
8. The deadline for submitting inquiries about the above-mentioned tender is 2025/03/20, provided they are submitted in Arabic (inquiries should be submitted to the Documents and Contracts Department <orig>إدارة الوثائق والعقود</orig> – Third Floor – Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> Headquarters – South Surra <orig>جنوب السرة</orig>), and no questions or inquiries received by the Authority <orig>المؤسسة</orig> after this date will be considered.

Second: The following conditions must be adhered to when submitting the bid:
1) The deadline for submitting bids (closing) is 1:00 PM at the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> Headquarters – South Surra <orig>جنوب السرة</orig> (Documents and Contracts Department <orig>إدارة الوثائق والعقود</orig> – Third Floor).
2) Proof of the company's execution and completion of similar works (the required similar works and their controls are detailed in item 'Third: Foundations and Criteria') as a main contractor during the last ten years (from the date of preliminary handover of the project) must be submitted, along with copies of the contract and a certificate of completion of works issued by the contracting entity.
3) The bidder must attach a clearance certificate stating that there are no impediments related to the labor registered with them at the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, in accordance with Circular No. (2) of 2021 issued by the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> on 2021/1/26.
4) A letter of authorization from the company in the name of the person authorized to submit the bid must be submitted, along with a copy of the civil ID of the same authorized person and a signature authentication certificate.

(5) The bidder must attach the preliminary bond with their bid, made out in favor of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig>, in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check, issued in Arabic, unconditional, free of any reservations, payable on demand, issued by a bank accredited in the State of Kuwait, and valid throughout the bid validity period and for the value specified in the above announcement. The bidder is not entitled to empty or seize it by any creditor or claim any interest thereon. Cash bonds will not be accepted. Any bid not accompanied by the preliminary bond shall be excluded.
(6) For local companies invited to participate in the tender and submitting their bids, their authorized representative shall place all tender documents and all required documents, complete, in their designated envelopes according to the instructions contained in the documents and the tender announcement, and seal them with red wax. They must personally, and under their personal responsibility, place the first envelope (bid submission envelope) in the designated box in the Documents and Contracts Department <orig>إدارة الوثائق والعقود</orig>, which contains:
- The preliminary bond (preliminary guarantee).
- The bid form and the total bid value (original copies), with complete data, stamped and signed.
- A certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, valid upon purchase of the tender.
(7) For international companies invited to participate in the tender and submitting their bids, their authorized representative shall place all tender documents and all required documents, complete, in their designated envelopes according to the instructions contained in the documents and the tender announcement, and seal them with red wax. They must personally, and under their personal responsibility, place the first envelope (bid submission envelope) in the designated box in the Documents and Contracts Department <orig>إدارة الوثائق والعقود</orig>, which contains:
- The preliminary bond (preliminary guarantee).
- The bid form and the total bid value (original copies), with complete data, stamped and signed.
- A registration certificate issued by the competent authorities in the country to which it belongs, stamped and signed by the official authorities in the country of incorporation, and attested by the Kuwaiti Consulate or any other entity authorized to attest (valid).

Third: Qualification Documents (Principles and Criteria): -
The bidder is committed to submitting all required documents proving their fulfillment of all conditions and requirements in the principles and criteria along with the bid documents, and placing them inside the envelope designated for the requirements of the principles and criteria as follows: -
Regarding local or foreign companies:
a. The company's capital must not be less than (5,000,000 K.D.) five million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
b. Submission of complete financial statements and data for the last three years, provided that the financial data are certified by an auditing firm and attested by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>, and certificates from the banks with which the bidder deals, indicating their financial position and the extent of the banks' readiness to provide facilities to them, provided that the certificates are valid and issued during the same year the tender was floated.
c. Submission of a list of projects completed of the same nature as the tender works (under the supply and installation system) as a main contractor during the last (10) years, provided that these projects are in the State of Kuwait, and that these projects have been in satisfactory efficient service for no less than (3) years.
d. The bidder must have successfully completed, as a main contractor, during the last (10) years, a contract for the implementation (supply and installation) of at least (1) main transformer station with a voltage of (400/132/11 kV) or a voltage of (300/132 kV) in the State of Kuwait (under the supervision of the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>), provided that this project included SF6 gas-insulated switchgear with a voltage of (400 kV) or a voltage of (300 kV) and at least (3) power transformers with a capacity of not less than (300 MVA). And that no more than (10) years have passed since the issuance of the Certificate of Receipt and Acceptance (Provisional Acceptance Certificate) for this project, and that this project has been in service for no less than (3) years.
OR the bidder must have successfully completed, as a main contractor, during the last (10) years, a contract/contracts for the implementation (supply and installation) of at least (1) main transformer station with a voltage of (132/33/11 kV) or a voltage of (132/11 kV) in the State of Kuwait (under the supervision of the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>). Provided that all these projects included SF6 gas-insulated switchgear with a voltage of (132 kV) and at least (3) power transformers with a capacity of not less than (30 MVA) each, and that no more than (10) years have passed since the issuance of the Certificate of Receipt and Acceptance (Provisional Acceptance Certificate) for this project, and that these projects have been in service for no less than (3) years.
e. The bidder must submit, in their capacity, all documents proving their fulfillment of all the above-mentioned clauses, including contract documents, certificates of receipt and acceptance, final certificates, and efficiency certificates from the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> proving their successful implementation of this/these project/projects and their entry into service for no less than (3) years.

Fourth: Rules and Conditions: -
1. The bidder must submit (3) CD copies of the required documents.
2. All submitted documents and papers must be certified and authenticated by the competent authorities and by the Embassy of the State of Kuwait in the country of origin to prove their authenticity and validity, and translated into Arabic by an accredited translation office.
3. All documents and data submitted by companies and institutions must be clear and sequential.
4. The Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> has the right to request any original copy to verify its conformity with the attached copies of the documents.
5. The bidder must submit a declaration and undertaking regarding the accuracy of the information and data provided with the bid submission.
6. The company is committed to filling out the table and submitting the required documents completely with the bid papers. In case of non-fulfillment of any of the clauses or required documents, the Authority has the right to exclude the bid.
7. All financial and legal documents will be subject to financial study and analysis to assess the company's financial capability and its eligibility to participate in the tender. The Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> has the right to reject any application if it does not meet the tender conditions.

Fifth:
This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.

Director General

The bid opening will be on the same closing day at 2:30 PM (14:30) on the Ground Floor - Theater.

Companies wishing to attend the bid opening meeting must send an email to PTS@zakathouse.Org.Kw one day before the bid opening, attaching (a letter from the company confirming the attendance of its representative - a copy of the civil ID). Please note that only one person from each company applying for the practice is allowed, and companies that do not comply will not be permitted to enter the bid opening meeting.
The validity period for bids for this practice is (90) days from the date of bid opening. The value of the preliminary insurance is two percent (2%) of the bid value, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee from one of the accredited local banks in Kuwait, valid for the duration of the bid and issued in the name of the bidder in favor of Zakat House / Bait Al-Zakat <orig>بيت الزكاة</orig>.

## Announcement of Extension of the Pre-qualification and Pre-qualification Update Period

In an effort to provide more time for business partners to meet all requirements, the Higher Purchasing Committee of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries announces the extension of the pre-qualification and pre-qualification lists update period for limited tenders, practices, and direct purchase orders through the unified electronic platform "K-Tendering" for an additional 45 days from the date of this announcement, in response to requests received from several companies.

### Invitation for Qualification and Qualification Update

Based on this extension, the Central Qualification Committee invites all commercial business partners to access the electronic platform "K-Tendering" via the following link:
https://ktendering.com.kw
to submit qualification applications or update qualifications as follows:
- **First:** Commercial entities wishing to qualify for the first time.
  - Submit qualification applications through the unified platform within an additional 45 days from the date of this announcement.
- **Second:** Previously qualified commercial entities.
  - If more than two years have passed since their qualification, they must submit qualification update applications within an additional 45 days from the date of this announcement.

### Qualification and Update Requirements

The application must include the following documents:
- Recent contracts and projects: documents proving the execution of similar works within the last ten years.
- Audited Financial Statements (AFS): issued by an independent auditor.

- The deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 27 March 2025, at 1:00 PM local time for the State of Kuwait (13:00 Noon), noting that bids must be submitted through the e-commerce platform mentioned above.
- The practitioner must submit the initial security in favor of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> in an envelope bearing the name and address of the practice and the closing date, and place it in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, at the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> main office building in Ahmadi, no later than 1:00 PM (13:00 Noon) on Thursday, 27 March 2025, with a copy of the initial security attached to the bid.
- The practitioner must deposit the practice document purchase fee into the account of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>, account number (KW59NBOK00000000000002004811204). Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be rejected. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid.
- Please note that this practice is indivisible, meaning that the supply must be from the unified qualification list of the Central Qualification Committee mentioned in the practice documents.
- No single person or group of persons acting jointly may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
- A person who has an interest in separate companies, each independent with its own legal personality, finances, employees, engineers, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies. Any bid from a tenderer violating this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders.
- Note:
  - All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the e-commerce platform as specified in the practice documents.
  - The Higher Purchasing Committee wishes to draw the attention of practitioners who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests

# Announcement

**RFQ-2142006**

Based on the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, the Higher Purchasing Committee for tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries announces the issuance of the above-mentioned tender, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the tender documents. Tender documents can be viewed or obtained, or any additional information can be found by visiting the unified electronic platform (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:

*   The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for depositing bids, and bids must be placed in a sealed envelope in the special bid box located at the company's headquarters – Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> Office Buildings Complex – Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> – Gate No. (1) – Building (B1) – Ground Floor.

*   Non-refundable.

*   This tender is general for all suppliers, non-divisible, provided that the required materials have been approved in the unified category of the Central Qualification Committee <orig>لجنة التأهيل المركزية</orig> as stated in the tender documents.
*   Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders: "No single person or group of persons collectively may register under more than one name during classification or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where tender conditions permit their submission. As for a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent in its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative bodies, he may, during classification, register himself and register each of his independent companies. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law."
*   The tenderer must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the tender number and company name to the purchase receipt issued by the bank and submitting the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be excluded. In case a copy of the payment receipt is submitted electronically with the bid:

**BANK NAME: NATIONAL BANK OF KUWAIT, AHMADI BRANCH**

The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for depositing and submitting bids, as detailed in the practice documents.

This practice is open to all suppliers, provided that spare parts are manufactured by AL-SHARHAN INDUSTRIES CO.W.L.L. KUWAIT and in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents.

- Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>: "No single person or group of persons collectively may register under more than one name during classification or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent in its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies during classification. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law."
- The practitioner <orig>الممارس</orig> must deposit the practice document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the practice number and company name to the purchase receipt issued by the bank and submitting the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by the payment receipt will be excluded. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached to the electronic bid:

Announcement

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that, in accordance with Article No. (33) and Article No. (88) of Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة رقم 2016/49</orig> regarding the subject of the aforementioned announcement, plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>. Therefore, all those wishing to view them should visit the website continuously to get the latest updates by following these steps:
1- Company Website WWW.KOCKW.COM
2- Click on E-business.
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFP's) and Purchases (RFQ's).
4- Click on Upcoming.
